TL;DR: 该研究探讨了星际介质中缺失氧元素的问题，提出通过远红外波段（44和62微米）观测结晶水冰特征来限制尺寸达5微米或更大的水冰颗粒含量，从而揭示部分缺失氧的存在形式，需高灵敏度和精确校准的远红外光谱仪进行探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 星际介质中约有四分之一的氧元素未被现有观测所解释，明确其存在形式对理解星际介质化学和恒星形成过程至关重要。

Method: 利用远红外波段（44和62微米）水冰的谱线特征，结合高灵敏度和高相对校准精度（优于1%）的光谱仪（如PRIMA/FIRESS），检测大尺寸水冰颗粒中的氧含量。

Result: 远红外观测可明确约束尺寸达5微米甚至更大的结晶水冰颗粒中的氧含量，弥补近红外方法在大颗粒探测上的不足。

Conclusion: 通过远红外波段的敏感观测，有望揭示星际介质中部分缺失氧以大尺寸水冰颗粒形式存在的证据，对星际化学和恒星形成研究具有重要意义。

Abstract: Study of interstellar elemental depletion poses an important problem in the
interstellar matter that at least a quarter of the total oxygen ($\sim 160$ ppm
relative to hydrogen) is not accounted for in any known form of oxygen in the
translucent or dense interstellar medium (ISM). Detailed analysis of the
absorption feature of water ice at 3 $\mu$m suggests that one fifth of the
missing oxygen may reside in 3 $\mu$m-sized water ice grains. However, the 3
$\mu$m feature becomes complex and weak for grains larger than 3 $\mu$m, and
thus the NIR spectroscopy is not the best means to study the presence of large
ice grains reliably. Here we show that sensitive observations of the
far-infrared (FIR) features of water ice at 44 and 62 $\mu$m enable us to
constrain the amount of crystalline water ice grains up to 5 $\mu$m or even
larger sizes unambiguously. Oxygen is one of the key elements in the ISM
chemistry, and [O I] 63 $\mu$m is a dominant cooling line in the neutral ISM.
Understanding the actual form of the missing oxygen in the ISM is crucial for
the study of the ISM and star-formation process. To detect the FIR features of
the crystalline water ice over the expected strong continuum, a sensitive FIR
spectrograph represented by PRIMA/FIRESS is indispensable. Since the feature is
broad, the low spectral resolution of $R \sim 130$ is sufficient, but accurate
relative calibration better than 1% is required.

Abstract: Striations are diffuse, linear, quasi-periodic, and magnetized structures

important role during the earliest stages of star formation. Theoretical models

### [184] [The Impact of Baryonic Effects on the Dynamical Masses Inferred Using Satellite Kinematics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.01690)
*Josephine F. W. Baggen,Frank C. van den Bosch,Kaustav Mitra*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种考虑重子效应的卫星星动力学解析模型，发现重子作用会降低视线速度弥散，导致推断的暗晕质量偏高，尤其在中等质量暗晕中影响可达5-8%，并提出校正方法，集成到BASILISK模型中，使中心星系的推断晕质量最高增加0.3 dex。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往研究忽略重子对卫星星动力学的影响，假设卫星仅在纯暗物质晕中运动，本文旨在量化重子（恒星、气体及暗物质的绝热响应）对动力学质量推断的影响。

Method: 构建包含恒星、气体及暗物质绝热响应的解析模型，覆盖10^12–10^15 M⊙暗晕质量范围，并依据观测标度关系和EAGLE模拟校准重子抛射与弥散恒星的质量分数，提出校正公式并集成至BASILISK贝叶斯推断框架。

Result: 重子效应主要导致卫星视线速度弥散降低，影响在10^12–10^13 M⊙暗晕中达5–6%，极端情况达8%；校正后中心星系的推断晕质量增加最多0.3 dex。

Conclusion: 重子效应对卫星动力学质量推断有显著影响，尤其在中等质量暗晕中不可忽略，需在校准星系-晕关联和宇宙学参数推断时加以考虑，同时为限制星系形成反馈效率提供了新途径。

Abstract: Satellite kinematics offers a powerful method to infer dynamical halo masses
and has been demonstrated to yield tight constraints on the galaxy-halo
connection. However, previous studies have assumed that the halos in which the
satellites orbit are composed solely of dark matter, neglecting the role of
baryons. Here, we develop an analytical model incorporating stars, gas, and the
adiabatic response of dark matter to assess the impact of baryonic effects on
the inference from satellite kinematics. The model covers halos in the mass
range $10^{12}-10^{15}M_\odot$ and is tuned to agree with well-established
observational scaling relations. In addition, the model uses simple functional
forms for the mass fractions of ejected baryons and diffuse halo stars,
calibrated to the median trends in the EAGLE hydrodynamical simulations. We
find that baryonic effects mainly result in a reduction of the satellite
line-of-sight velocity dispersion due to the ejection of baryons and the
resulting response of the dark matter halo. The effect is minimal (less than
1%) for the most massive halos, but reaches ~5-6% for halos in the mass range
$10^{12}-10^{13}M_\odot$, and up to 8% in extreme cases. We propose a simple
formalism for correcting the satellite line-of-sight velocity dispersion for
baryonic effects, and for marginalizing over the uncertainties. We integrate
this correction function into BASILISK, a Bayesian hierarchical inference
method applied to satellite kinematics data extracted from large redshift
surveys, and find that this shifts central galaxies to higher inferred halo
masses at fixed luminosity by up to ~0.3 dex. In a forthcoming work, we
demonstrate that these few-percent level baryonic effects can have a
non-negligible impact on the inference of cosmological parameters, motivating a
novel approach to constraining the efficiency of feedback processes associated
with galaxy formation.

</details>

*Carlotta Gruppioni,Lee Armus,Matthieu Bethermin,Laura Bisigello,Denis Burgarella,Francesco Calura,Ivan Delvecchio,Andrea Enia,Andreas Faisst,Francesca Pozzi,Giulia Rodighiero,Alberto Traina,Livia Vallini*

Method: 利用Spitzer-IRAC和ALMA的深场观测识别高红移大质量暗星系，并计划通过PRIMA/PRIMAger在25-265微米波段的成像覆盖JWST与ALMA之间的光谱空白，结合FIRESS的中远红外光谱观测，探测细结构谱线以研究其尘埃性质和ISM物理。

Abstract: One of the main open issues in galaxy formation and evolution is the early
assembly of the most massive galaxies and their contribution to the stellar
mass and star formation rate densities at early epochs. Massive red sources
already in place at z > 2 to 3 have been found in deep Spitzer-IRAC and ALMA
surveys. They are often called optically and near-IR dark, or HST-dark, being
undetected even in the deepest HST frames. The submillimeter (i.e., ALMA)
detection of these sources confirms their high-z dusty nature: they are massive
(e.g., log(M*/Msun) > 10) and dusty star-forming galaxies with estimated
redshifts in the 2.5 to 7 range. They seem to lie mostly below the main
sequence (MS) of star-forming galaxies and show gas depletion times <1 Gyr.
Imaging with the PRIMA/PRIMAger instrument over the full 25 to 265 micron range
will allow us to characterize their still uncovered spectral energy
distributions between JWST and ALMA spectral windows, probing their dust
content and properties (e.g., temperature, mass), whereas spectroscopic
observations with FIRESS will be the key to investigate the nature of their
powering source (e.g., AGN or star formation) and to study the physics of their

### [186] [Supermassive black hole growth from stellar binary encounters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.02316)
*Aubrey Jones,Benjamin C. Bromley*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文研究了超大质量黑洞通过希尔机制吸积恒星的增长过程，利用模型预测了不同星系环境中黑洞的增长情况，并在30个星系中发现了两个可能通过此机制近期增长的候选体。此外，来自大麦哲伦云的超高速星观测结果暗示了双星与黑洞相互作用可能是其黑洞增长的重要途径。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用一个基于恒星中心密度、速度弥散、双星比例和黑洞质量等参数的模型来预测恒星捕获率，并估计不同星系环境中超大质量黑洞的增长情况。

Abstract: The growth of supermassive black holes (SMBHs) remains a central problem in
astrophysics, with current observations providing only limited constraints on
the underlying mechanisms. One possible growth channel is stellar accretion via
the Hill's mechanism, wherein a SMBH tidally breaks up a passing binary star,
capturing and eventually accreting a member of the binary. We adopt a model to
predict capture rates from parameters that include the central number density
of stars, the stellar velocity dispersion, the binary fraction, and black hole
mass. We then use this model to estimate the growth of SMBHs across a range of
galactic environments. In a data set of 30 galaxies of various types and
masses, we identify two candidates with SMBHs for which stellar accretion may
be a driver of recent growth. Closer to home, a recent analysis of observed
hypervelocity stars from the Large Magellanic Cloud (LMC) implicates binary
star interactions with a massive black hole. Every hypervelocity star produced
in this way leaves a bound partner that may be accreted, providing an active
growth channel for the LMC's black hole.

### [187] [Multiple star-forming episodes of intermediate-redshift galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.01710)
*C. Muñoz López,Davor Krajnović,B. Epinat,T. Urrutia,I. Pessa,T. Contini,T. Nanayakkara,J. Pharo,T. S. Gonçalves,Tran Thi Thai,N. F. Bouché*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 该研究分析了393个中等红移星系的恒星形成历史，发现大多数星系经历了多次恒星形成事件，且大质量星系比小质量星系更早完成恒星形成并进入静止状态，其早期恒星形成事件在宇宙早期（约z~3时）已完成，并贡献了大部分恒星质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究中等红移星系在不同环境下的恒星形成历史及其演化规律，理解星系质量与恒星形成活动之间的关系。

Method: 通过建模恒星形成率（SFR），量化并表征星系的恒星形成事件（SFEs）次数，并分析其平均年龄、金属丰度、SFR等参数在不同环境和质量下的变化趋势。

Result: 超过85%的星系经历了一次以上的恒星形成事件；大质量星系的恒星形成事件更少，形成更快，且其早期恒星形成事件持续时间更长，通常在z~3时已完成；场星系与群星系在质量、金属丰度、恒星年龄和形成时标上存在显著差异，但不同群环境之间无明显相关性。

Conclusion: 星系的恒星形成历史与其质量密切相关，大质量星系更早完成恒星形成，而小质量星系经历更复杂的多阶段形成过程；环境对星系演化的影响较弱，主要差异体现在场与群之间。

Abstract: We derive and analyse the star formation histories of 393
intermediate-redshift (0.1 $\leq$ z $\leq$ 0.9) galaxies with stellar masses
between $\sim$10$^{8}$ - 10$^{12}$ M$_{\odot}$. We probe a cosmic time of
approximately 6 Gyr and a range of environments, from field (low-density
systems) to rich groups (high-density systems). We find that the galaxies'
stellar mean ages, metallicities, and star formation rates (SFRs) follow
similar trends to galaxies as those characterising the nearby Universe. We
modelled the derived SFRs, quantifying and characterising the number of
star-forming episodes (SFEs). We found that more than 85$\%$ of the galaxies
have more than one event of star formation, typically described with an
exponentially decaying SFR and subsequent Gaussian-like episode(s) of star
formation. We also observe that massive galaxies have fewer SFEs than low-mass
systems and that they form their stellar mass and reach quiescence faster than
lower mass galaxies. Moreover, the history of mass assembly for the most
massive galaxies in the sample can be described with only one episode of star
formation in the early Universe, which we detected as an exponential decrease
that was longer in duration than subsequent SF events. This early event has
typically been completed by z$\sim$3 and it accounts for a high fraction of the
total stellar mass, from $\sim$40$\%$ for low-mass galaxies to more than 50$\%$
for higher-mass galaxies. We also analysed the dependence of stellar population
parameters with the various environments probed by the sample, finding no
significant correlations between different group environments; however, our
field galaxies are generally distinct from group galaxies in terms of the mass,
metallicity, stellar ages, and formation timescales. We discuss possible biases
in the sample selection and examine how representative our galaxies are of the
overall galaxy population.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用VLT/MUSE窄场模式的自适应光学辅助数据，在~50 pc分辨率下拟合三轴轨道动力学模型，并结合高灵活性的光谱拟合技术分析恒星运动学与化学特性。

Abstract: We present a dynamical and chemical study of the centre of a massive
early-type strong-lens galaxy ESO286-G022 (SNL-1). Analysing new data obtained

mass-to-light ratio expected for a Kroupa-like IMF. We also employ a

Abstract: We present new JWST/NIRCam observations of the interacting dwarf galaxy
system NGC 4485/NGC 4490 (a.k.a. Arp 269), obtained as part of the Cycle 1
Feedback in Emerging extrAgalactic Star clusTers (FEAST) program. NGC 4485 and
NGC 4490 form the closest known pair of interacting late-type dwarf galaxies
(at $\sim 7.4$ Mpc), excluding the Magellanic Clouds. Near-infrared
color-magnitude diagrams (CMDs) reveal a wide range of stellar populations in
both galaxies, including young ($\lesssim 200$ Myr) upper main sequence stars,
core helium-burning stars, and oxygen-rich asymptotic giant branch (AGB) stars.
We also identify intermediate-age ($\sim 200$ Myr -- $1$ Gyr) carbon-rich AGB

CMDs show two distinct bursts of star formation beginning $\sim 30$ Myr and
$\sim 200$ Myr ago, the latter consistent with the most recent pericenter
passage predicted by N-body simulations. The spatial distribution of stars
reveals a tidal bridge extending from NGC 4485 and connecting to the disk of
NGC 4490. Compact star-forming regions are seen along NGC 4490's spiral arms,
possibly originating from its infrared nucleus. A significant metallicity
gradient is observed in the young stellar populations forming the bridge. These
findings suggest that during the last pericenter passage, gas was stripped from
NGC 4485 via tidal forces or ram pressure, accreted by NGC 4490, and mixed with
in-situ material, fueling ongoing star formation. This system provides a unique
nearby laboratory for studying how tidal interactions shape the star formation
and chemical enrichment history of dwarf galaxies.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于约3300个星系的光谱红移样本，使用Prospector SED拟合代码和灵活的尘埃模型，分析UV-optical消光曲线斜率。

Abstract: The UV-optical dust attenuation curve is key to interpreting the intrinsic
properties of galaxies and provides insights into the nature of dust grains and
their geometry relative to stars. In this work, we constrain the UV-optical
slope of the stellar attenuation curve using a spectroscopic-redshift sample of
~3300 galaxies at z~1-9, to characterize the diversity and redshift evolution
of stellar attenuation curves and to gain insight into dust production and
evolution at high redshifts. The sample is constructed from three JWST/NIRCam
grism surveys in GOODS and A2744 fields, with a wealth of JWST/NIRCam and HST
photometry. With constraints from spectroscopic redshifts and emission line
fluxes, we use the Prospector SED fitting code with a flexible dust model. We
find that the attenuation curve slope varies strongly with Av at all redshifts,
becoming flatter at higher attenuation. We find no strong correlation between
attenuation curve slope and size or axis ratio, and the trends with stellar
mass and star-formation rate are largely driven by their correlation with Av.
We find strong evidence that at fixed Av, the curve becomes flatter with
increasing redshift. On average, the attenuation curves derived here are
shallower than those at z~0 and than the SMC curve. The highest redshift
galaxies at z=7-9 (124 galaxies, a significantly larger sample than in previous
studies) show slopes even flatter than the Calzetti curve, implying reduced UV
obscuration and lower IR luminosities than expected from an SMC dust curve, by
as large as an order of magnitude. Hydrodynamical simulations that couple dust
growth to gas chemical enrichment successfully reproduce the different loci of
high- and low-redshift galaxies in the slope-Av diagram, suggesting that dust
in high-redshift galaxies is increasingly dominated by large grains produced in
supernova ejecta with limited ISM processing at early times.

### [191] [Relating spatially resolved optical attenuation, dust and gas in nearby galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.01803)
*E. D. Paspaliaris,S. Bianchi,E. Corbelli,A. Concas*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用CIGALE SED拟合代码绘制尘埃质量和消光面密度图，并结合FUV到亚毫米波段观测、原子与分子气体面密度图以及光学积分场光谱数据，逐像素独立估计巴尔末减缩消光。

Result: 发现尘埃面密度和巴尔末减缩消光更好地追踪分子和总气体面密度；年轻恒星的SED消光与巴尔末减缩消光一致；老恒星消光符合标准银河盘混合模型，而年轻恒星消光介于前景尘埃屏与混合构型之间。

Abstract: We relate the optical attenuation inferred by the Balmer decrement,
$A_{V\mathrm{,BD}}$, and by the SED-fitting, $A_{V\mathrm{,SED}}$, to the dust
distribution and gas surface density throughout the disc of galaxies, down to
scales smaller than 0.5 kpc. We investigate five nearby star-forming spirals
with available FUV to sub-mm observations, along with atomic and molecular gas
surface density maps and optical integral-field spectroscopic data. We use the
CIGALE SED-fitting code to map the dust mass surface density
($\Sigma_\mathrm{dust}$) and $A_{V,\mathrm{SED}}$ of different stellar
populations. For each pixel, we independently estimate the attenuation from the
BD.
  We find that both $\Sigma _\mathrm{dust}$ and $A_{V,\mathrm{BD}}$ trace
better the molecular and total gas mass surface density, rather than the atomic
gas. Since regions sampled in this study have high molecular fractions, atomic
gas surface densities, indicative of molecular gas shielding layers, decrease
as the mean dust-to-gas ratio increases from galaxy to galaxy. The fitted
attenuation towards young stars, $A^\mathrm{young}_{V,\mathrm{SED}}$, is in
good agreement with $A_{V,\mathrm{BD}}$ and it can then be used to trace the
attenuation in star forming galaxies where integral-field observations are not
available. We estimate the ratio of $A_{V,\mathrm{BD}}$ over the total stellar
$A_{V,\mathrm{SED}}$ and find it slightly larger than what has been found in
previous studies. Finally, we investigate which dust distribution reproduces
better the estimated $A_{V,\mathrm{BD}}$ and $A_{V,\mathrm{SED}}$. We find that
the attenuation towards old stars is consistent with the expectations for a
standard galactic disc, where the stellar and dust distributions are mixed,
while $A_{V, \mathrm{BD}}$ and the $A^\mathrm{young}_{V, \mathrm{SED}}$ are
between the values expected for a foreground dust screen and a mixed
configuration.

</details>


### [192] [The ALMA-QUARKS survey: Extensive detection of acetamide in multiple high-mass star-forming regions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.01904)
*Chunguo Duan,Xuefang Xu,Qian Gou,Tie Liu,Laurent Pagani,Fengwei Xu,Ke Wang,Xunchuan Liu,Jun Kang,Mingwei He,Jiaxiang Jiao*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究利用ALMA Band 6数据对52个热分子核进行了乙酰胺（CH₃CONH₂）的首次系统性搜寻，成功在10个核中探测到乙酰胺，显著扩展了已知的乙酰胺发射源。乙酰胺与甲酰胺的丰度比和强相关性表明二者可能存在关联的表面化学形成路径，支持其在星际环境中与前生命化学的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 乙酰胺作为关键的星际酰胺分子及其前生命意义此前因探测稀少而受限，研究旨在系统探测其在热分子核中的分布，以揭示其形成机制及在前生命化学中的潜在作用。

Method: 利用ALMA Band 6对52个热分子核进行乙酰胺的系统性光谱巡天，结合谱线拟合与辐射转移模型推导柱密度，并与甲酰胺丰度进行相关性分析。

Result: 在10个热分子核中成功探测到乙酰胺，柱密度范围为(2.5±0.9)×10¹⁴ 至 (1.5±0.6)×10¹⁶ cm⁻²；与甲酰胺的丰度比稳定在3–9之间，且存在强相关性，提示二者可能通过尘埃颗粒表面化学过程共同形成。

Conclusion: 乙酰胺在大质量恒星形成区中较为普遍，其与甲酰胺的化学关联支持表面形成机制，且复杂有机分子可在恒星形成过程中存续，为前生命化学演化提供了重要线索。

Abstract: Acetamide (CH$_{3}$CONH$_{2}$), a key interstellar amide and a methyl
derivative of formamide (NH$_{2}$CHO), has been sparsely detected, limiting
insights into its prebiotic relevance. We present the first systematic survey
for acetamide toward 52 hot molecular cores using ALMA Band 6 data. Acetamide
has been detected in 10 cores, markedly expanding the inventory of known
emitters. The derived column densities of acetamide range from
$(2.5\pm0.9)\times10^{14}$ to $(1.5\pm0.6)\times10^{16}$ cm$^{-2}$, compared to
formamide's $(1.1\pm0.1)\times10^{15}$ to $(6.9\pm0.4)\times10^{16}$ cm$^{-2}$.
The nearly constant abundance ratios (~3-9) and strong abundance correlation
between the two amides across sources suggest a chemically linked formation
pathway, likely on grain surfaces. The presence of peptide-like molecules in
these regions implies that complex organic species can survive star formation
processes, offering a potential pathway toward prebiotic chemistry. These
findings constrain the dominant grain surface formation routes of acetamide,
confirm its broader prevalence in highmass star-forming regions, and underscore
the importance of targeted amide surveys in tracing the chemical evolution
toward prebiotic complexity.

### [193] [Investigations of MWISP Clumps: 13CO Clump Source Catalog and Physical Properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.01955)
*Yu Jiang,Qing-Zeng Yan,Ji Yang,Sheng Zheng,Xuepeng Chen,Yang Su,Zhibo Jiang,Zhiwei Chen,Xin Zhou,Yao Huang,Xiaoyu Luo,Haoran Feng,De-Jian Liu*

TL;DR: 本文通过MWISP项目的数据，利用改进的检测算法提取了71,661个13CO分子云核，并提出自动化的距离判定方法，解决了运动学距离模糊问题，为研究银河系分子云核性质和恒星形成提供了重要基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在构建银河系内分子云核的完整样本，解决距离模糊问题，以研究其物理性质、恒星形成活动及在银河系演化中的作用。

Method: 开发了结合FacetClumps算法的全局检测方案，并设计了基于信号区域的自动分层距离判定方法，应用于MWISP一期高分辨率13CO数据立方体（覆盖2310 deg²）。

Result: 成功提取71,661个分子云核，97.94%获得可靠距离；统计显示65.3%云核具有引力束缚，贡献约96.3%的总质量；发现云核群体具有普适的幂律标度关系，且与脉泽相关的云核表现出不同的参数分布和标度关系。

Abstract: We present the first comprehensive catalogs of $^{13}$CO clumps from the
Milky Way Imaging Scroll Painting (MWISP) project. By developing an equivalent
global detection scheme integrated with the FacetClumps algorithm, we
successfully extract 71,661 molecular clumps across a high-resolution $^{13}$CO
data cube spanning 2310 deg$^2$ from the MWISP Phase I survey. To determine
accurate distances, we design an automatic hierarchical distance decision
method using signal regions as fundamental objects, effectively resolving the
kinematic distance ambiguity problem and obtaining reliable measurements for
97.94% of the sample. Statistical analysis reveals that 65.3% of clumps are
gravitationally bound, accounting for approximately 96.3% of the statistical
total mass. Scaling relation analysis across multiple surveys reveals universal
power-law behaviors in clump populations. Maser-associated clumps exhibit
modified parameter distributions and scaling relations, revealing how active
star formation alters clump dynamics and structure. These extensive catalogs
establish a foundation for investigating molecular clump properties, star
formation processes, and Galactic evolution.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析远红外尘埃发射谱能量分布的斜率，研究其对局部辐射场估计和不同尘埃成分丰度的依赖性，并评估PRIMA高光谱成像和偏振观测的潜力。

Conclusion: PRIMA的高光谱成像和偏振观测能力将有助于克服当前建模局限，实现对M31星系中尘埃成分比例更精确且空间分辨的测量。

Abstract: The properties of interstellar dust grains are being scrutinized more than
ever before, with the advent of large facilities. Infrared emission from dust
grains is a powerful asset than can help constrain their physical and chemical
properties. Among these, the relative ratio of carbon-rich to silicate-rich
grains remains one that has not yet been investigated thoroughly, due to the
lack of dedicated instruments and modeling limitations. In this paper, we
quantify the modeling degeneracies inherent to constraining the far-infrared
(far-IR) slope of the dust emission spectral energy distribution. Used as a
proxy for the silicate-to-carbon ratio, we find that recovering the far-IR
slope is affected by the estimate of the local radiation field, and the input
abundances of different grain species. We show that PRIMA's Hyperspectral
Imaging will lead to better constrained local radiation fields which will aid
-- together with PRIMA's polarization capabilities -- to better constrain the
silicate-to-carbon ratio in M31, and how it spatially varies within the galaxy.

### [195] [A bar stability criterion distinguishing between modified gravity and dark matter in galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.02016)
*Tahere Kashfi,Mahmood Roshan,Virginia Cuomo,Benoit Famaey,Asiyeh Habibi,Srikanth T. Nagesh*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 该研究基于ELN稳定性准则，通过统计分析和N体模拟，探讨了在星系尺度上区分暗物质与修正牛顿动力学（MOND）的可能性，发现在无气星系中两者在条形不稳定性上存在可观测差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在检验暗物质与MOND在星系尺度上的可区分性，特别是在条形结构形成稳定性方面。

Method: 利用SPARC和CALIFA数据库验证ELN稳定性准则的统计有效性，并通过N体模拟比较暗物质和MOND框架下的条形不稳定性行为。

Result: ELN准则成功识别约70%的有条形星系；N体模拟显示，在满足ELN稳定条件的暗物质模型中星系稳定，而在MOND下出现条形不稳定性。

Conclusion: 在无气星系中，暗物质与MOND在条形形成稳定性上表现出可观测差异，暗示可通过稳定性行为区分二者，但MOND中抑制条形形成机制需进一步研究外部场效应。

Abstract: This paper presents a study on the distinguishability of dark matter and
Modified Newtonian Dynamics (MOND) at galactic scales based on the stability
criterion proposed by Efstathiou, Lake, and Negroponte (ELN criterion). First,
we test the statistical validity of this stability criterion against the
presence of bars within the SPARC and CALIFA databases, successfully
identifying $\sim 70\%$ of barred galaxies. Then, we employ a series of N-body
galaxy simulations to exhibit a direct observable difference between the dark
matter and MOND theoretical frameworks, at least in gas-poor galaxies. We
present N-body models that satisfy the stability requirement of the ELN
criterion, and so are stable against bar formation in the presence of a dark
matter halo, and that do actually exhibit bar instabilities in MOND. On the
other hand, the question of how to inhibit bar formation in gas-poor galaxies
in MOND is posed, and requires a detailed investigation of the external field
effect.

### [196] [Detection of 'super-virial' gas in the Circumgalactic medium of the Milky Way towards PKS 2155-304](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.02019)
*Mukesh Singh Bisht,Sanskriti Das,Smita Mathur,Manami Roy,Yair Krongold,Anjali Gupta*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 首次在PKS 2155-304方向上利用Chandra和XMM-Newton光谱探测到银河系CGM中四种不同电离相的吸收特征，包括首次探测到MgXII Kα线，揭示了热、温热、温和冷四个相共存，并显示超晕、晕和次晕气体在南北半球均广泛分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索银河系星周介质（CGM）中高温电离气体的相结构和化学成分，验证此前仅在北半球观测到的热气体是否在南半球也存在，以确定其空间分布的普遍性。

Method: 利用Chandra和XMM-Newton的高分辨率光栅光谱，对blazar PKS 2155-304方向的吸收线进行分析，结合非模型依赖方法和混合电离模型，识别不同温度相并推断其物理和化学性质。

Result: 探测到MgXII Kα和SiXIV Kα吸收线，确认CGM中存在四个明确温度相：热超晕（~5.4×10⁷ K）、温热晕（~1.8×10⁶ K）、温次晕（~2.2×10⁵ K）和冷相（<1.7×10⁵ K）；发现不同电离态元素丰度差异，且低电离线蓝移、高电离线红移，暗示多相气体流动结构。

Conclusion: 银河系CGM中存在多相高温气体，且超晕热气体在南半球同样存在，表明其在全天空广泛分布，支持CGM中存在复杂流入、静止和外流动力学结构。

Abstract: We present the first simultaneous detection of four distinct highly ionized
$z=0$ absorbing phases using Chandra and XMM-Newton grating spectra toward the
blazar PKS 2155$\hbox{-}$304. We detect the MgXII K$\alpha$ absorption line for
the first time in the circumgalactic medium (CGM) of the Milky Way. Along with
MgXII K$\alpha$, we detect SiXIV K$\alpha$ absorption, which are the tell-tale
signatures of the hot 'super-virial' gas in the CGM. Both from the
model-independent calculations and hybrid-ionization modeling, we infer four
phases at distinct temperatures, hot 'super-virial' ($5.4^{+1.9}_{-0.8} \times
10^7$ K), warm-hot 'virial' ($1.8^{+0.3}_{-0.2} \times 10^6$ K), warm
'sub-virial' ($2.2\pm 0.5 \times 10^5$ K), and cool phase ($<1.7 \times 10^5$
K). The warm-hot and hot phases are $\alpha$-enhanced, and [C/O] and [Ne/O] are
super-solar in the warm-hot phase, while [Mg/O] and [Si/O] are super-solar in
the hot phase. The low-ionization lines are blue-shifted (v$_{\rm los} \approx
-100$ km s$^{-1}$), whereas the high-ionization lines are red-shifted. It
suggests a scenario of infalling sub-virial, quasi-static virial, and
outflowing super-virial phases along this sightline. Earlier studies on
individual sightlines were confined to the Northern Hemisphere. Our sightline
is located in the Southern hemisphere, demonstrating that hot super-virial gas
is also present at Southern Galactic latitudes as well. This confirms a more
widespread distribution of the super-virial gas across both hemispheres.

### [197] [The ALPINE-CRISTAL-JWST Survey: Revealing Less Massive Black Holes in High-Redshift Galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.02027)
*Wenke Ren,John D. Silverman,Andreas L. Faisst,Seiji Fujimoto,Lin Yan,Zhaoxuan Liu,Akiyoshi Tsujita,Manuel Aravena,Rebecca L. Davies,Ilse De Looze,Miroslava Dessauges-Zavadsky,Rodrigo Herrera-Camus,Edo Ibar,Gareth C. Jones,Jeyhan S. Kartaltepe,Anton M. Koekemoer,Yu-Heng Lin,Ikki Mitsuhashi,Juan Molina,Ambra Nanni,Monica Relano,Michael Romano,David B. Sanders,Manuel Solimano,Enrico Veraldi,Vicente Villanueva,Wuji Wang,Giovanni Zamorani*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究利用JWST/NIRSpec IFU在18个高红移恒星形成星系中系统搜索宽线活动星系核（AGN），发现7个AGN候选体，其中1个高度可靠，6个具宽线成分，部分处于并合系统中。研究表明仅靠窄线诊断易遗漏AGN，宽线探测更有效。AGN占比5.9%–33%，可能因目标星系质量较高。这些候选体黑洞质量为10^6–10^7.5 M⊙，光度接近或低于本地M_BH-M⋆关系，提示此前发现的超大质量黑洞可能存在选择偏差。JWST揭示了高红移下大量欠质量AGN的存在，强调需考虑质量依赖的选择效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高红移星系中识别AGN常受限于诊断方法的模糊性，尤其是窄线诊断图中星系与AGN重叠区域难以区分。此前JWST研究发现黑洞质量超出于宿主星系的趋势，可能存在选择偏差。因此，需通过更有效的手段（如宽线探测）系统搜寻AGN，以理解AGN与宿主星系的共同演化及其在早期宇宙中的真实占比。

Method: 利用JWST/NIRSpec积分视场单元（IFU）对18个高红移（z=4.4–5.7）、高恒星质量（M⋆>10^9.5 M⊙）的恒星形成星系进行观测，提取33个光度峰中心的光谱，搜索宽Hα发射线。通过线宽（FWHM）识别宽线AGN候选体，并结合窄线诊断图分析其分类可靠性，估算AGN分数并推断黑洞质量与光度。

Result: 共识别出7个宽线AGN候选体：1个高度可靠（FWHM~2800 km/s），6个具宽成分（FWHM~600–1600 km/s），其中两个位于并合系统。这些源在窄线诊断图中无法区分，凸显宽线探测的重要性。AGN分数为5.9%–33%，黑洞质量为10^6–10^7.5 M⊙，光度比L_bol/L_Edd ~ 0.1–1。与此前研究不同，这些候选体接近或低于本地M_BH-M⋆关系，表明以往结果可能受选择偏差影响。

Conclusion: 本研究证实JWST能够有效揭示高红移星系中以往被遗漏的低光度宽线AGN，表明在高质星系样本中AGN比例较高。这些AGN的黑洞质量符合或略低于本地标度关系，挑战了此前‘超大质量黑洞’的普遍性结论，强调了质量依赖的选择偏差在AGN搜寻中的关键作用。结果支持存在大量欠质量AGN，正被JWST逐步探测到，为早期宇宙中黑洞与星系共演化提供了新视角。

Abstract: We present a systematic search for broad-line active galactic nuclei (AGNs)
in the ALPINE-CRISTAL-JWST sample of 18 star-forming galaxies
($M_\star>10^{9.5}~M_{\odot}$) at redshifts $z=4.4-5.7$. Using JWST/NIRSpec
IFU, we identify 7 AGN candidates through the detection of broad \Ha\ emission
lines from 33 aperture spectra centred on photometric peaks. These candidates
include one highly robust AGN detection with FWHM $\sim$ 2800 \kms\ and six
showing broad components with FWHM $\sim 600-1600$ \kms, with two in a merger
system. We highlight that only broad-line detection is effective since these
candidates uniformly lie within narrow emission-line ratio diagnostic diagrams
where star-forming galaxies and AGNs overlap. The broad-line AGN fraction
ranges from 5.9\% to 33\%, depending on the robustness of the candidates.
Assuming that the majority are AGNs, the relatively high AGN fraction is likely
due to targeting high-mass galaxies, where simulations demonstrate that
broad-line detection is more feasible. Their black hole masses range from
$10^6$ to $10^{7.5}~M_{\odot}$ with $0.1 \lesssim L_{\rm bol}/L_{\rm
Edd}\lesssim 1$. Counter to previous JWST studies at high redshift that found
overmassive black holes relative to their host galaxies, our candidates lie
close to or below the local $M_{\rm BH}-M_\star$ scaling relations, thus
demonstrating the effect of selection biases. This study provides new insights
into AGN-host galaxy co-evolution at high redshift by identifying faint
broad-line AGNs in galaxy samples, highlighting the importance of considering
mass-dependent selection biases and the likelihood of a large population of
AGNs being undermassive and just now being tapped by JWST.

### [199] [SDSS J1001+5027: Strong microlensing-induced chromatic variation caught in the act](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.02169)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We conducted long-term monitoring of the doubly imaged gravitationally lensed
quasar SDSS J1001+5027 consisting of spectro-photometric observations separated
by $\sim$120 days (time delay between both quasar images), as well as test and
auxiliary data. This monitoring approach allowed us to reliably find a strong

to very promising observations of the system in the coming years. These future

information to discuss, among other things, the structure of the inner

### [200] [Primordial black holes in the main lensing galaxy of FBQ 0951+2635](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.02193)
*Daniel Isla,Luis J. Goicoechea,Ana Esteban-Gutiérrez,Vyacheslav N. Shalyapin,Rodrigo Gil-Merino,Jose M. Diego,Eleana Ruiz-Hinojosa*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文研究了双像引力透镜类星体FBQ 0951+2635的主透镜星系中可能存在的原初黑洞（PBHs）种群，通过16年的微引力透镜变异性观测数据与90种不同物理情景的模拟信号进行对比，发现长期变异性支持小质量分数的PBHs存在，并对木星质量和约10倍太阳质量的PBHs的质量分数提供了限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索星系中暗物质的组成，特别是原初黑洞作为暗物质候选者的可能性。

Method: 假设星系质量由平滑分布物质、恒星和原初黑洞共同构成，利用16年观测到的微引力透镜变异性数据与90种不同物理情景下的模拟信号进行详细比较。

Result: 虽然所考虑的情景均无法完全复现整体观测信号，但长期变异性倾向于支持小质量分数的原初黑洞存在；同时，若能获得基于回响映射的较小源尺寸测量，则可对木星质量级别的原初黑洞质量分数施加强约束；要限制约10倍太阳质量的原初黑洞质量分数，可能需要五倍长度的光变曲线。

Conclusion: 长期微引力透镜变异性数据支持星系中存在小质量分数的原初黑洞，且未来更长时标的观测有助于进一步约束大质量原初黑洞的比例。

Abstract: Although dark matter in galaxies may consist of elementary particles
different from those that make up ordinary matter and that would be smoothly
distributed (still undetected), the so-called primordial black holes (PBHs)
formed soon after the initial Big Bang are also candidates to account for a
certain fraction of mass in galaxies. In this paper, we focused on the main
lensing galaxy ($z$ = 0.260) of the doubly imaged gravitationally lensed quasar
FBQ 0951+2635 ($z$ = 1.246) for probing possible PBH populations. Assuming that
the mass of the galaxy is due to smoothly distributed matter (SDM), stars, and
PBHs, the 16-yr observed microlensing variability was compared in detail with
simulated microlensing signals generated by 90 different physical scenarios.
Among other details, the simulated signals were sampled as the observed one,
and the observed variability in its entirety and over the long term were used
separately for comparison. While none of the scenarios considered can reproduce
the overall observed signal, the observed long-term variability favours a small
mass fraction in PBHs with a mass of the order of the mean stellar mass.
Furthermore, it is possible to obtain strong constraints on the galaxy mass
fraction in Jupiter-mass PBHs, provided that a reverberation-based measurement
of the source size is available and relatively small. To constrain the mass
fraction in $\sim$10 $\rm{M_{\odot}}$ PBHs, light curves five times longer are
probably required.

### [201] [Signal Drop in Magnification Profiles: Combining Lensing Simulations and Observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.02213)
*David Crespo,Joaquín González-Nuevo,Laura Bonavera,Marcos M. Cueli,Hu Zou,Rebeca Fernández-Fernández,Jose M. Casas*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究引力透镜放大偏差测量中质量密度轮廓的信号下降现象，评估卫星星系在其中的作用。

Method: 采用堆叠技术分析星系团中卫星星系的径向分布，通过角交叉相关测量背景亚毫米星系的放大偏差，并利用引力透镜模拟器解释结果。

Result: 卫星星系分布在大尺度上符合NFW轮廓，但在内区超出该模型；未在约10角秒处发现类似透镜测量中的信号下降，表明中心大质量星系的强透镜效应可能抑制了预期信号，形成了“爱因斯坦间隙”。

Conclusion: 卫星星系的分布与引力透镜导出的质量密度轮廓相关，但中心星系的强透镜效应显著影响信号，需在未来的质量轮廓估计中加以考虑。

Abstract: Gravitational lensing magnification bias is a valuable tool for studying mass
density profiles, with submillimetre galaxies (SMGs) serving as ideal
background sources. The satellite distribution in galaxy clusters also provides
insights into their mass distribution.This study aims to investigate the signal
drop in mass density profiles from magnification bias measurements, assessing
the role of satellite galaxies through observational data and lensing
simulations. Using a stacking technique, we analyze the radial distribution of
satellites in clusters and measure the magnification bias on background SMGs
via angular cross-correlations. A gravitational lensing simulator aids in
interpreting the results. Our analysis confirms that satellite distributions
align with a Navarro-Frenk-White profile on large scales but exceeding it in
the inner part. However, the lack of a similar signal drop at $\sim$10
arcseconds as in the lensing measurements suggests a strong lensing effect from
massive central galaxies. The study provides new insights into the mass density
profiles derived from gravitational lensing and their relation to satellite
distributions within galaxy clusters. The introduction of a gravitational
lensing simulator helps explain the emergence of an ``Einstein Gap'' induced by
strong lensing effects associated to a change in the apparent position of the
sources that suppresses the expected signal. These findings provide a deeper
understanding of how satellite galaxies influence gravitational lensing and
offer a framework for improving mass density profile estimations in future
studies.

### [202] [A High Incidence of Mid-infrared Variability in Local Ultraluminous Infrared Galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.02254)
*Shun Hatano,Masatoshi Imanishi,Takanobu Kirihara,Takashi Yamamoto,Yuxing Zhong,Chenghao Zhu*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 利用NEOWISE近11年的中红外测光数据，研究了30个本地超亮红外星系（ULIRGs）的中红外变异性，发现其变化可能源于潮汐瓦解事件（TDEs）或活动星系核（AGN）环结构的内在变化，表明中红外变异性是探测被尘埃遮蔽AGN的有效手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索ULIRGs中中红外（MIR）波段的变异性，以揭示其变源本质，特别是区分超新星、TDEs和AGN的贡献。

Method: 基于NEOWISE多历元目录中约11年的WISE测光数据，识别具有显著MIR变异性的ULIRGs，并分析其光变幅度、时标及可能的物理机制。

Result: 发现30个显著MIR变源，其W2波段光变幅度ΔL_W2为7×10^42至5×10^44 erg/s，其中25个超过已知超新星的MIR光度上限，且多数具有AGN活动迹象，表明变因更可能为TDEs或AGN环变化。

Conclusion: MIR变异性是探测被尘埃遮蔽AGN的有效工具，揭示了ULIRGs中强烈的核活动，大多数变异源与AGN相关，即使由TDE引起，也发生在已有AGN的星系中。

Abstract: We explore mid-infrared (MIR) variability in local ultraluminous infrared
galaxies (ULIRGs; infrared luminsoity $L_{\rm IR}>10^{12}\ L_\odot$) utilizing
the $\sim$11 years of photometry from the NEOWISE multi-epoch catalog of {\it
Wide-field Infrared Survey Explorer} ({\it WISE}). We identify 30 variable
ULIRGs with statistically significant MIR variability. The variability is
observed on timescales of a few years, implying that the MIR-emitting regions
are compact ($\lesssim 1$ pc). The difference between maximum and minimum $W2$
(4.6 ${\rm \mu}$m) band luminosity ($\Delta L_{\rm W2}$) of the 30 variable
ULIRGs range from $\Delta L_{W2}$ = $7\times10^{42}$ to $5\times 10^{44}$ erg
s$^{-1}$. The $\Delta L_{W2}$ of 25 variable ULIRGs out of 30 are greater than
$\Delta L_{W2}$ = $1\times10^{43}$ erg s$^{-1}$, surpassing the MIR luminosity
{range} observed in known supernovae (SNe; $L_{\rm 3.6\ {\rm \mu m}}$ and
$L_{\rm 4.5\ {\rm \mu m}}$ < 10$^{42.3}$ erg s$^{-1}$). Therefore, the MIR
variabilities in these 25 ULIRGs are most likely driven by tidal disruption
events (TDEs) or intrinsic changes in their active galactic nuclei (AGN) torus
emission. Our sample includes hard X-ray detected AGNs (e.g., UGC 05101) and
previously reported TDE candidates (IRAS F01004-2237, IRAS 05189-2524). All 25
also exhibit at least one AGN signature(s) besides the MIR variability,
suggesting that even if the MIR variability originates from TDEs, the black
holes responsible are likely AGNs. Our results suggest that MIR variability is
an effective tool for detecting buried AGNs and highlights the intense nuclear
activity in ULIRGs.

*Macarena Uribe,Sandro Villanova,Douglas Geisler,José G. Fernández-Trincado,Cesar Muñoz,Nicolás Barrera,Thaiz Pino,Franco Sepúlveda*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对银晕中严重消光的球状星团Terzan 2进行详细的化学丰度和动力学分析，填补高消光区域星团研究的空白，并探讨其多星族特征及在银河系演化中的位置。

Method: 利用APOGEE-2S光谱仪获取高分辨率近红外光谱，采用BACCHUS代码进行逐线元素丰度分析，并结合动力学模拟研究轨道特性。

Result: 测得Terzan 2的平均金属丰度[Fe/H] = -0.84 ± 0.04，无内在铁丰度弥散；C和N存在显著变化，表明存在多星族；α元素富集趋势与银河系球状星团一致；动力学分析显示其轨道混沌，受银心棒影响但未被捕获。

Abstract: We present the first detailed spectroscopic analysis of the heavily extincted
bulge globular cluster Terzan 2 (Ter 2) based on high-resolution near-infrared
spectra obtained as part of the CAPOS (the bulge Cluster APOgee Survey)
project. CAPOS focuses on surveying clusters within the Galactic Bulge, using
the APOGEE-2S spectrograph, part of the SDSS-IV survey, a component of the
second generation Apache Point Observatory Galactic Evolution Experiment
(APOGEE-2). For the spectral analysis, we use the Brussels Automatic Code for
Characterizing High accUracy Spectra (BACCHUS) code which provides line-by-line
elemental abundances. We derive abundances for Fe-peak (Fe, Ni), $\alpha$-(O,
Mg, Si, Ca, Ti), light-(C, N), odd-Z(Al), and the s-process element (Ce) for
four members of the cluster. Our analysis yields a mean metallicity of [Fe/H]=
$-$0.84 $\pm$ 0.04, with no evidence for an intrinsic variation. We detect a
significant abundance variation only in C and N, indicating the presence of
multiple populations. Ter 2 exhibits a typical $\alpha$-enrichment, that
follows the trend of Galactic GCs. Additionally, our dynamical analysis reveals
that Terzan 2 is a bulge globular cluster with a chaotic orbit that is
influenced by the Galactic bar but not trapped by it, displaying both prograde
and retrograde motions within the inner bulge region. Overall, the chemical
patterns observed in Terzan 2 are in good agreement with those of other CAPOS
bulge clusters of similar metallicity.

### [204] [How far have metals reached? Reconciling statistical constraints and enrichment models at Reionization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.02434)
*Sebastian Lopez,Jens-Kristian Krogager*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 该论文通过红移参数化方法研究了Mg II和O I吸收系统的宇宙演化，发现冷气体在星系晕中的分布随时间减少，且强吸收系统与恒星形成率同步增长至宇宙正午时期。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解类星体吸收系统中低电离物种（如Mg II和O I）的宇宙演化及其与星系形成和金属富集过程的关系。

Method: 利用吸收截面与星系空间密度的比例关系，结合红移参数化统计模型，拟合低红移Mg II等效宽度数据，并外推至再电离时期到宇宙正午时期的演化。

Result: 1. Mg II吸收范围在z≈6–8后持续减小，尤其在弱吸收系统中更明显，O I受影响更大；2. 强吸收系统线密度随恒星形成率增至宇宙正午达峰，弱系统则保持稳定或下降；3. 再电离结束时，风尚未影响邻近晕，支持自富集模型。

Conclusion: 观测统计支持半解析模型关于早期金属富集的观点，为z>6的吸收线研究提供了实用比较基准。

Abstract: The incidence of quasar absorption systems and the space density of their
galaxies are proportional, the proportionality factor being the mean absorbing
cross section. In this paper we use redshift parameterizations of these two
statistics to predict the cosmic evolution of an equivalent-width ($W_r$)
radial profile model, tailored for the low-ionization species Mg II and O I.
Our model provides an excellent match with well-sampled, low-redshift Mg II
equivalent-width/impact-parameter pairs from the literature. We then focus on
the evolution of various quantities between the Reionization and Cosmic Noon
eras. Our findings are: (1) The extent of Mg II and hence the amount of cool
($T\sim 10^4$ K), enriched gas in the average halo decreases continuously with
cosmic time after $z \approx 6$--$8$. This effect is more pronounced in
$W_r^{2796}\lesssim 0.3$ {\AA} systems (outermost layers of the model) and, in
general, affects O I more than Mg II, probably due to the onset of
photoionization by the UV background. (2) The line density of
$W_r^{2796}\gtrsim 1$ {\AA} systems (model inner layers) constantly increases
in synchrony with the star formation rate density until it reaches a peak at
Cosmic Noon. The line density of $W_r^{2796}\lesssim 0.3$ {\AA} systems, on the
other hand, remains constant or decreases over the same period. (3) At the end
of Reionization, the filling factor is low enough that the winds have not yet
reached neighboring halos. This implies that the halos are self-enriched, as
suggested by semi-analytic models. We discuss how these statistical predictions
can be reconciled with early metal enrichment models and offer a practical
comparison point for future analyses of quasar absorption lines at $z>6$.

</details>

Abstract: The integrated luminosity from the features of the polycyclic aromatic
hydrocarbons (PAHs) exceeds the luminosity from atomic and molecular emission
lines in the star-forming regions in galaxies and is a potential tracer of
galaxy-scale star formation and molecular gas content of the high-redshift
universe. We simulate the observable PAH spectra using the PRobe far-Infrared
Mission for Astrophysics far-infrared enhanced survey spectrometer (FIRESS) and

### [206] [PRIMA Vista: far-infrared polarimetry to unveil small-scale magnetohydrodynamics in extragalactic observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.02533)
*Diego Maglione,Sergio Martin-Alvarez,Enrique Lopez-Rodriguez,Susan E. Clark,Kaitlyn Karpovich*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Magnetic fields are a fundamental part of the interstellar medium (ISM) and
remain a challenge for building a comprehensive understanding of galactic
properties. Their study requires far-infrared polarimetric observations, which
provide an unrivaled probe of the dynamics, magnetization, and structure of the
coldest and densest interstellar gas and dust at small scales in galaxies,
where mass and star formation reside. We use high-resolution
magnetohydrodynamical simulations of a face-on Milky Way-like galaxy and show
that the alignment of magnetic fields with ISM structures and the turbulence at
100 pc scales decrease with increasing magnetization. We make predictions for
extragalactic observations by the proposed PRobefarInfrared Mission for
Astrophysics (PRIMA) telescope, comparing them with Stratospheric Observatory
For Infrared Astronomy (SOFIA) observations similar to those of the Survey of
extragALactic magnetiSm with SOFIA (SALSA). PRIMA will be able to better
measure magnetic alignment trends inaccessible by SOFIA. We find that PRIMA
will better sample magnetic turbulence, especially in dense environments, and
will be able to measure the unresolved intrinsic magnetic field orientations to
approximately 6 deg precision. PRIMA will also be capable of resolving
observables such as the polarized fraction or the magnetic alignment down to
scales comparable to the resolution of our simulations (about 10 pc) for
galaxies up to 0.5 Mpc away. The polarization-dispersion relation shows that
PRIMA observations will suffer from significantly reduced beam depolarization.
Furthermore, PRIMA will recover the correlation between increasing the magnetic
alignment parameter and local polarization fraction. Overall, observations of
local galaxies with PRIMA will better characterize interstellar magnetism and
constrain ISM and galaxy models, advancing our understanding of magnetism in
the universe.

### [207] [Chemodynamics of BoötesI with $S^{5}$: Revised Velocity Gradient, Dark Matter Density, and Galactic Chemical Evolution Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.02546)

Motivation: 旨在利用更大、空间分布更广的恒星样本，改进对Boo I星系系统性质、动力学特征、金属丰度梯度及暗物质分布的理解，并探究其可能的潮汐起源和星系演化历史。

Method: 结合S5巡天和存档光谱数据，识别成员星并测量速度与金属丰度；首次在UFD中修正视向旋转效应；采用轴对称Jeans模型拟合暗物质密度分布；使用单区星系化学演化模型重新分析金属丰度分布函数。

Result: 获得了148颗成员星，探测到4σ显著性的视线速度梯度（1.2±0.3 km/s/r_h），发现金属丰度梯度为-0.10±0.02 dex/r_h，暗物质密度轮廓弱偏好有核的（cusped）分布（γ=1.0^{+0.5}_{-0.6}），并推断出快速但低效的恒星形成及强烈的星系外流。

Conclusion: Boo I存在与轨道对齐的速度梯度，可能源于潮汐作用；其金属丰度梯度与先前研究一致；暗物质分布倾向于有核模型；其恒星形成历史短暂且效率低，伴随强烈外流，反映了早期星系演化特征。

Abstract: We combine new spectroscopic observations of the ultra faint dwarf galaxy
(UFD) Bo\"otes I (Boo I) from the Southern Stellar Stream Spectroscopic Survey
($S^{5}$) with $\sim$15 years of archival spectroscopic data to create the
largest sample of stellar kinematics and metallicities to date in any Milky Way
UFD. Our combined sample includes 148 members extending out to $\sim$7
half-light radii ($r_h$), including 24 newly confirmed members, 18 binary
candidates, 15 RR Lyrae stars, and 92 [Fe/H] measurements. Using this larger
and more spatially extended sample, we provide updated constraints on Boo I's
systemic properties, including its radial population gradients. Properly
accounting for perspective rotation effects in a UFD for the first time, we
detect a $4\sigma$ line-of-sight velocity gradient of $1.2\pm0.3$ km s$^{-1}$
$r_h^{-1}$ aligned along Boo I's orbit and discuss its potential tidal origins.
We also infer a metallicity gradient of $-0.10\pm0.02$ dex $r_h^{-1}$ in
agreement with previous studies. Using an axisymmetric Jeans model, we provide
updated constraints on Boo I's dark matter density profile, which weakly favor
a cusped ($\gamma=1.0^{+0.5}_{-0.6}$) dark matter profile. Lastly, we
re-analyze Boo I's metallicity distribution function with a one-zone galactic
chemical evolution model and place new constraints on its rapid, inefficient
star formation and strong galactic outflows.

</details>


### [208] [Is feedback-free star formation possible?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.02566)
*A. Ferrara,D. Manzoni,E. Ntormousi*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: Lyα辐射压力在超新星爆发前阶段显著限制恒星形成效率，消除‘无反馈’恒星形成模式的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨在超新星反馈之前是否存在无反馈的高效恒星形成阶段，以及Lyα辐射压力对此过程的影响。

Method: 通过理论分析和乐观假设下的辐射流体动力学模拟，研究Lyα光子辐射压力对不同气体面密度云中恒星形成效率的影响。

Result: 在考虑Lyα辐射压力的情况下，云的恒星形成效率ε*普遍低于0.08；在乐观假设下，效率随气体面密度增加而上升，最高达到0.27，但仍低于0.4。

Conclusion: Lyα辐射压力强烈限制恒星形成效率，即使在太阳金属丰度下也消除了ε*≳0.4的无反馈恒星形成模式的存在可能性。

Abstract: It has been suggested that, if the free-fall time of star-forming clouds is
shorter than the lifetime ($\approx 3 $ Myr) of massive stars exploding as
supernovae (SN), a large fraction of the cloud gas can be converted into stars
during an allegedly `feedback-free' phase. Here, we show that radiation
pressure from Ly$\alpha$ photons produced in the pre-SN phase can instead erase
feedback-free conditions, and severely limit the star formation efficiency
(SFE). We find that, for a constant star formation rate, all clouds with gas
surface density $(37-1.7 \times 10^5)\ M_\odot\ \rm pc^{-2}$ have $\epsilon_* <
0.08$. Higher SFE values can only be reached if Ly$\alpha$-driven shells
fragment and form stars. While advanced RHD simulations are required to
establish the importance of this effect, adopting an optimistic guess, we find
that the SFE increases with cloud surface density, rising from
$\epsilon_*=0.023$ at $\Sigma_g = 37\ M_\odot\ \mathrm{pc^{-2}}$ to
$\epsilon_*=0.27$ at $\Sigma_g = 1.7 \times 10^5\ M_\odot\ \mathrm{pc^{-2}}$.
Given the optimistic assumptions adopted, these numbers should be regarded as
upper limits. We conclude that Ly$\alpha$ radiation pressure strongly limits
the SFE, even at solar metallicities, erasing the possibility that a
feedback-free star formation mode with $\epsilon_* \gtrsim 0.4$ exists in the
pre-SN phase. This conclusion remains valid even when other effects such as
dust destruction of Ly$\alpha$ photons, presence of HII regions, velocity
gradients, atomic recoil, and turbulence are considered.

</details>

### [209] [Signals of Bursts from the Very Early Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.00237)
*Leo Stodolsky,J. Silk*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文探讨了早期宇宙爆发事件可能产生的可观测信号，如中微子脉冲等，并分析了这些信号如何传播到宇宙微波背景辐射时期或被早期吸收，可能导致的可观测效应包括对CMB局部区域的影响、由正电子产生引起的软X射线以及对遗迹中微子背景的非热贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究早期宇宙中剧烈时空扰动（如大质量黑洞或婴儿宇宙形成）可能产生的可观测信号，以探索宇宙极早期的物理过程。

Method: 分析来自早期宇宙的脉冲如何逃逸或被吸收，讨论其对宇宙微波背景辐射、软X射线和遗迹中微子背景的潜在影响。

Result: 发现这些脉冲可能在CMB上留下局部效应，产生可探测的软X射线信号，或增加遗迹中微子背景的非热成分。

Conclusion: 尽管早期宇宙爆发产生的直接信号难以探测，但它们可能通过间接方式留下可观测印记，为研究极早期宇宙提供新途径。

Abstract: We consider possible observable signals from explosive events in the very
early universe, ``bursts". These could be expected in connection
  with massive black hole or ``baby universe'' formation. We anticipate that
such major disruptions of spacetime would be associated with
  neutrino and perhaps other pulses. While these seem to be not
  detectable directly, we discuss how they could lead to potentially observable
signals. We analyze how the pulses from very early times
  may ``escape'', that is
  propagate to the last scattering epoch at the time $t_{cmb}$ and later,
  or alternatively be absorbed earlier, ``contained''. The possibly detectable
signals include effects on small regions of the CMB, a soft x-ray resulting
from positron production, or a nonthermal addition to
  the relic neutrino background.

</details>


### [210] [Looking beyond lambda](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.00359)
*Alexie Leauthaud,Adam Riess*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 近年来的观测数据揭示了ΛCDM模型在描述宇宙膨胀历史方面的局限性，暗示暗物质和暗能量可能比现有模型更复杂，需超越简单假设，探索更复杂的暗区物理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ΛCDM模型在解释宇宙微波背景、重子声学振荡和局部校准的Ia型超新星等观测数据时出现不一致，促使研究者重新审视标准宇宙学模型的适用性。

Method: 通过分析现有高精度观测数据（如CMB、BAO和SNe Ia），评估ΛCDM模型的局限性，并倡导采用新设施和新研究策略来探索暗区物理。

Result: 现有数据表明暗区可能具有更复杂的物理机制，仅测试w=-1已不足以描述暗能量行为，需发展更丰富的理论框架。

Conclusion: 应准备进入后ΛCDM时代，推动对暗物质、暗能量和引力的深入理解，同时改进科研实践以应对未来挑战。

Abstract: Widening cracks are appearing in the $\Lambda$CDM model and it is becoming
increasingly clear that the standard cosmological model struggles to describe
the full expansion history of the Universe as revealed by the Cosmic Microwave
Background, Baryon Acoustic Oscillation measurements, and locally calibrated
Type Ia supernovae. Taken at face value, recent results suggest a dark sector
that may be more complex than commonly assumed. We must prepare for the
possibility of moving beyond the $\Lambda$CDM era, where merely testing $w=-1$
is no longer sufficient, and embrace the challenge of unraveling the physics of
dark matter, dark energy and gravity on cosmic scales. Guided by increasingly
robust data - secured through considerable investment - we should pursue deeper
understanding while being open to complexity in the dark sector, rather than
settling for the simplest phenomenology. New data from new facilities and a new
dark energy task force could help illuminate the path forward while changes to
our scientific practices will be essential to navigate the potentially rocky
road ahead.

### [211] [Bubble in bubbles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.00758)
*Dongdong Wei,Zong-Kuan Guo,Qiqi Fan*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 研究了宇宙相变中双层真空泡的演化与形成，发现飞越跃迁可在克服势垒后稳定形成双层泡，而量子效应在某些条件下无法形成此类结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索多真空宇宙相变中双层真空泡的形成机制及其与传统单壁泡的差异。

Method: 采用半经典方法结合初始速度涨落，并通过数值模拟研究泡壁加速、碰撞及被困区域的形成。

Result: 飞越跃迁可稳定形成双层真空泡，其动力学行为与单壁泡显著不同，影响引力波产生和重子生成等可观测量。

Conclusion: 飞越跃迁是传统量子隧穿之外的一种补充衰变机制。

Abstract: We investigate the evolution and formation of double-layered vacuum bubbles
during cosmological phase transitions with mltiple vacua. Using a semiclassical
approach with initial velocity fluctuations, we demonstrate that under certain
conditions, quantum effects do not lead to the formation of double-layered
vacuum bubbles, while flyover transitions allow for their stable formation by
overcoming successive potential barriers. The evolution of these bubbles,
including wall acceleration, collisions, and the formation of trapped regions,
is explored through numerical simulations. Our results show that the dynamics
of double-layered bubbles differ significantly from standard single-wall
bubbles, with implications for cosmological observables such as gravitational
wave production and baryogenesis. These findings indicate that flyover
transitions represent a complementary decay mechanism to the conventional
quantum tunneling process.

</details>


### [212] [Emulating Global 21 cm Cosmology Observations from the Lunar Far Side to Achieve Quick and Reliable Physical Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.00976)
*J. Dorigo Jones,J. O. Burns,D. Rapetti,Shah Mohammad Bahauddin,B. Reyes,D. W. Barker*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文开发了基于LSTM和KAN的神经网络模拟器（21cmLSTM和21cmKAN），用于高效、准确地模拟宇宙早期中性氢的21厘米信号，支持快速的贝叶斯参数推断，其中21cmKAN在保持高精度的同时训练速度提升75倍，可在30分钟内完成端到端训练与推断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于基于物理模型的21厘米信号模拟在贝叶斯多参数推断中计算成本高昂，亟需高效的模拟工具以应对即将到来的月球背面射电望远镜观测数据。

Method: 提出并实现了两种基于神经网络的模拟器：21cmLSTM利用长短期记忆网络捕捉信号的时间相关结构，21cmKAN则通过学习表达性强的函数变换实现快速训练。

Result: 21cmLSTM是目前社区中最准确的模拟器，21cmKAN在保持相似精度的同时训练速度快75倍，两者均能拟合真实模拟信号并给出无偏的物理参数约束，且21cmKAN可在30分钟内完成端到端训练与推断。

Conclusion: 将此类机器学习工具集成到数据分析流程中，对充分利用未来宇宙学21厘米信号观测至关重要。

Abstract: Efforts are underway to measure the global 21 cm signal from neutral
hydrogen, which is a powerful probe of the early universe, using NASA radio
telescopes on the far side of the Moon. Physics-based models of the signal are
computationally expensive to perform Bayesian multi-parameter inferences, for
which we have developed novel, publicly-available neural network emulators
utilizing a Long Short-Term Memory (LSTM) network and a Kolmogorov-Arnold
Network (KAN). $\texttt{21cmLSTM}$ is currently the most accurate emulator in
the community by leveraging the signal's temporally-correlated structure, and
$\texttt{21cmKAN}$ maintains similar accuracy while training 75 times faster,
by learning expressive functional transformations. Each emulator can fit
realistic mock signals and obtain unbiased physical parameter constraints, with
$\texttt{21cmKAN}$ able to complete end-to-end training and inference in under
30 minutes. The implementation of machine learning tools like these in data
analysis pipelines is important to fully exploit upcoming measurements of the
cosmological 21 cm signal.

</details>


### [213] [An SIDM simulation of the merging cluster El Gordo and its tension between the post collision DM density profiles and weak lensing constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.01298)
*R. Valdarnini*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文通过模拟和弱引力透镜数据分析了星系团El Gordo的并合过程，发现自相互作用暗物质模型可解释观测到的质量成分偏移，但与现有上限冲突，且无法解释引力剪切剖面的发散行为，提示需探索新的暗物质物理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨在高能星系团碰撞中暗物质是否具有碰撞特性，并检验自相互作用暗物质模型在解释观测现象中的有效性与局限性。

Method: 结合包含自相互作用暗物质的并合模拟与弱引力透镜观测数据，分析质量成分空间偏移、视线方向速度差异及密度轮廓特征。

Result: 发现自相互作用暗物质模型（σ_DM/m_X ~ 4–5 cm²/g）可再现质量成分偏移和数百km/s的恒星速度差，但该截面值超出当前星系团尺度上限；后碰撞暗晕具核心密度轮廓（r_c ~ 300 kpc），预测剪切信号在小角度趋零，与观测到的NFW型发散行为矛盾。

Conclusion: 现有自相互作用暗物质模型难以同时解释所有观测特征，需更复杂的物理机制；这种张力可作为探测新暗物质物理的独特实验平台。

Abstract: We review recent findings from a detailed simulation study of the merging
cluster El Gordo and present new results inferred from weak lensing data. We
found that the observed spatial offsets between the different mass components
are well reproduced in merging simulations that include self-interacting dark
matter (DM), with an elastic cross-section per unit mass of approximately
\sigma_DM/m_X ~ 4 -5 cm^2/gr. Moreover, a relative line-of-sight peculiar
velocity on the order of several hundred km/s is found between the two stellar
components of the colliding subclusters. These findings strongly suggest the
possibility that, in a very energetic cluster collision, DM could possess
collisional properties. However, the self-interacting DM merger model presented
here is not without difficulties. The values found for \sigma_DM/m_X being in
conflict with the current upper bounds on cluster scales. As a solution to this
tension we argue that in major cluster mergers the physical modeling of DM
interactions, based on the scattering of DM particles, should be considered too
simplistic. Additionally, the DM halos of the post-collision clusters have
cored density profiles with core radii r_c ~ 300 kpc. Consequently, the
associated reduced tangential shear lensing profiles consistently tend to zero
at angles \theta <~ 40^{''}. This result is inconsistent with what is deduced
from the measured profiles. These profiles exhibit a diverging behavior when
\theta --> 0, as predicted by an NFW mass model. We argue that such
contradictions cannot be easily reconciled within the DM models presented so
far as an alternative to the collisionless paradigm. However, we suggest that
this tension can be used as a unique test bed to probe new DM physics.

</details>


### [214] [Les Houches on Dark Universe 2025: Elements of cosmology beyond FLRW](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.01320)
*Pierre Fleury*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文讨论了严格应用宇宙学原理所导致的FLRW模型在描述宇宙膨胀动力学和光传播运动学方面的表现，并探讨了所谓的反作用和拟合问题。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于宇宙学原理，分析FLRW模型在宇宙动力学和光传播中的应用，并讨论反作用和拟合问题。

Result: 展示了FLRW模型在预测宇宙膨胀和观测解释方面的性能，并提出了反作用和拟合问题的相关结果。

Conclusion: FLRW模型作为宇宙学背景模型具有重要作用，但其在严格应用下面临反作用和拟合等挑战。

Abstract: Modern cosmology is based on the cosmological principle, which states that
the Universe is statistically homogeneous and isotropic. When applied in its
strict -- rather than statistical -- sense, the cosmological principle leads to
the Friedmann--Lema\^itre--Robertson--Walker (FLRW) model, which serves as
background spacetime. This background is used to predict: (1) the dynamics of
cosmic expansion; and (2) the kinematics of light propagation through the
Universe, which dictates the interpretation of cosmological observations. In
this lecture, we shall discuss the performance of the FLRW model for those
purposes, and present some results on the so-called backreaction and fitting
problems.

</details>


### [215] [An Accurate Comprehensive Approach to Substructure: IV. Dynamical Friction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.01553)
*Eduard Salvador-Solé,Alberto Manrique,Andreu Rocamora*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文在先前工作的基础上，通过引入动力摩擦（DF）效应，以完全解析的方式重新分析了暗晕子结构的丰度和径向分布，成功解释了模拟结果，并推广到任意质量、红移和形成时间的暗晕。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前的研究忽略了动力摩擦对暗晕子结构的影响，为了更准确地解释模拟结果并提升理论模型的完整性，需要将动力摩擦纳入分析框架。

Method: 采用峰值模型和嵌套峰值统计（无自由参数）结合子晕剥离与激波加热的物理模型（仅一个参数），以完全解析的方式引入动力摩擦，避免对子晕轨道运动进行数值积分。

Result: 得到了不同质量子晕的丰度和径向分布的简单而精确的解析表达式，成功分离了动力摩擦与潮汐剥离、激波加热的效应，重现并解释了数值模拟结果。

Conclusion: 动力摩擦在子结构演化中起着重要作用，该解析模型能准确描述子晕分布，并可推广至任意宇宙学参数、质量和红移下的暗晕系统。

Abstract: In three previous Papers we analysed the origin of the properties of halo
substructure found in simulations. This was achieved by deriving them
analytically in the peak model of structure formation, using the statistics of
nested peaks (with no free parameter) plus a realistic model of subhalo
stripping and shock-heating (with only one parameter). However, to simplify the
treatment we neglected dynamical friction (DF). Here, we revisit that work by
including it. That is done in a fully analytic manner, i.e. avoiding the
integration of subhalo orbital motions. This leads to simple accurate
expressions for the abundance and radial distribution of subhaloes of different
masses, which disentangle the effects of DF from those of tidal stripping and
shock-heating. This way we reproduce and explain the results of simulations and
extend them to haloes of any mass, redshift and formation times in the desired
cosmology.

</details>


### [216] [The Perfect Host: JWST Cepheid Observations in a Background-Free SN Ia Host Confirm No Bias in Hubble-Constant Measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.01667)
*Adam G. Riess,Siyang Li,Gagandeep S. Anand,Wenlong Yuan,Louise Breuval,Stefano Casertano,Lucas M. Macri,Dan Scolnic,Yukei S. Murakami,Alexei V. Filippenko,Thomas G. Brink*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: JWST观测对Ia型超新星宿主星系中的造父变星进行了高分辨率测量，特别是在低背景污染的NGC 3447系统中，验证了HST数据中不存在显著的光度偏差，支持造父变星距离的可靠性，并测得H₀ ≈ 73 km/s/Mpc，与ΛCDM模型预测存在~6σ差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验HST数据中造父变星测距是否存在因分辨率不足导致的光度偏差，以验证哈勃常数（H₀）测量的可靠性，并探究Hubble张力是否源于系统误差。

Method: 利用JWST Cycle 1和Cycle 2对19个Ia型超新星宿主星系（>50%样本）中的>100颗造父变星进行高分辨率近红外观测，特别选取背景污染极低的NGC 3447系统进行三重对比（HST、JWST、无背景干扰），分析光度偏差与弥散。

Result: 在NGC 3447中未发现组件间系统偏移（σ<0.03 mag），背景自由条件下弥散降至0.12 mag；全样本中未发现JWST与HST之间的显著偏差；结合JWST与HST数据测得H₀ = 73.49 ± 0.93 km/s/Mpc，加入TRGB校准后为H₀ = 73.18 ± 0.88 km/s/Mpc。

Conclusion: 造父变星测距在高分辨率下依然可靠，光度偏差不足以解释Hubble张力，观测支持当前H₀测量结果与ΛCDM模型之间存在显著差异。

Abstract: Cycle 1 JWST observations of Cepheids in SN Ia hosts resolved their
red-giant-dominated NIR backgrounds, sharply reducing crowding and showing that
photometric bias in lower-resolution HST data does not account for the Hubble
tension. We present Cycle 2 JWST observations of >100 Cepheids in NGC 3447, a
unique system that pushes this test to the limit by transitioning from low to
no background contamination. NGC 3447, an SN Ia host at D~25 Mpc, is an
interacting pair comprising (i) a spiral with mixed stellar populations,
typical of H0 calibrators, and (ii) a young, star-forming companion (NGC 3447A)
devoid of old stars and hence stellar crowdinga rare "perfect host" for testing
photometric bias. We detect ~60 long-period Cepheids in each, enabling a
"three-way comparison" across HST, JWST, and background-free conditions. We
find no component-to-component offset (sigma<0.03 mag; a calibration
independent test), and a 50% reduction in scatter to ~0.12 mag in the
background-free case, the tightest seen for any SN Ia host. Across Cycles 1-2
we also measure Cepheids in all SH0ES hosts observed by JWST (19 hosts of 24
SNe Ia; >50% of the sample) and find no evidence of bias relative to HST
photometry, including for the most crowded, distant hosts. These observations
constitute the most rigorous test yet of Cepheid distances and provide strong
evidence for their reliability. Combining JWST Cepheid measurements in 19 hosts
(24 SNe Ia) with HST data (37 hosts, 42 SNe Ia) yields H0 = 73.49 +/- 0.93
km/s/Mpc. Including 35 TRGB-based calibrations (from HST and JWST) totals 55
SNe Ia and gives H0 = 73.18 +/- 0.88 km/s/Mpc, ~6 sigma above the LambdaCDM+CMB
expectation.

</details>


### [217] [Probing the Dark Sector using the Fornax Satellite](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.01713)
*Eyal Zamlung,Adi Nusser*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 研究暗物质与重子之间弱等效原理（WEP）破缺的观测特征，通过N体模拟表明，当第五力强度β≳0.6时，会显著剥离恒星成分，与观测不符；而β≲0.2时与现有观测基本一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索暗物质与重子之间弱等效原理破缺的可能性及其对卫星星系结构的影响。

Method: 使用N体模拟一个类似Fornax的银河系卫星星系，引入相对于牛顿引力强度为β的暗区第五力（屏蔽长度远大于银河系晕尺寸），研究其对恒星与暗物质分布的影响。

Result: 当β≳0.6时，大部分恒星成分被剥离，无法重现Fornax的观测特征；当β≲0.2时，恒星剥离较弱，模拟结果与当前光度和运动学观测基本一致。

Conclusion: 暗区长程力若过强（β≳0.6）会导致与观测不符的结构演化，较弱的力（β≲0.2）则仍可接受，为暗区第五力提供了观测约束。

Abstract: A long-range force acting only in the dark sector can displace the stellar
component of satellite galaxies relative to their dark matter (DM) halos,
thereby \emph{breaking} the weak equivalence principle (WEP) between DM and
baryons. We investigate observational signatures of such WEP breaking using
$N$-body simulations of a Fornax-like Milky Way (MW) satellite, implementing a
fifth force between DM particles of amplitude $\beta$ relative to Newtonian
gravity (with a screening length much larger than the MW halo size). We find
that $\beta \gtrsim 0.6$ strips and unbinds the bulk of the stellar component,
leaving at most a negligible bound remnant that fails to match the observed
stellar content, surface-brightness, and line-of-sight velocity-dispersion
profiles of Fornax. By contrast, $\beta \lesssim 0.2$ yields only mild stellar
stripping and remains broadly consistent with current photometric and kinematic
constraints within our modeling assumptions.

### [218] [One latent to fit them all: a unified representation of baryonic feedback on matter distribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.01881)
*Shurui Lin,Yin Li,Shy Genel,Francisco Villaescusa-Navarro,Biwei Dai,Wentao Luo*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 提出了一种统一的二维潜在表示方法，用于准确且简洁地量化重子反馈对物质分布的影响，该表示独立于时间和宇宙学，维度更低且可解释性强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于不同星系形成模拟模型及其子网格物理参数化之间的巨大差异，精确且简洁地量化重子反馈对物质分布的影响具有挑战性。

Method: 利用来自4种不同模型的5072个模拟数据，在广泛的参数空间中寻找统一的二维潜在表示，并分析其对物质功率谱的影响。

Result: 发现了一个与时间和宇宙学无关、低维且解耦的二维潜在空间，能够清晰区分黑洞和超新星反馈对物质功率谱的不同影响，并实现了不同模型间参数空间的可比性。

Conclusion: 该方法为从观测数据中提取物理信息提供了鲁棒且高效的分析模型，具有推广到其他存在显著建模不确定性的领域的潜力。

Abstract: Accurate and parsimonious quantification of baryonic feedback on matter
distribution is of crucial importance for understanding both cosmology and
galaxy formation from observational data. This is, however, challenging given
the large discrepancy among different models of galaxy formation simulations,
and their distinct subgrid physics parameterizations. Using 5,072 simulations
from 4 different models covering broad ranges in their parameter spaces, we
find a unified 2D latent representation. Compared to the simulations and other
phenomenological models, our representation is independent of both time and
cosmology, much lower-dimensional, and disentangled in its impacts on the
matter power spectra. The common latent space facilitates the comparison of
parameter spaces of different models and is readily interpretable by
correlation with each. The two latent dimensions provide a complementary
representation of baryonic effects, linking black hole and supernova feedback
to distinct and interpretable impacts on the matter power spectrum. Our
approach enables developing robust and economical analytic models for optimal
gain of physical information from data, and is generalizable to other fields
with significant modeling uncertainty.

### [219] [Alignment of spiral and elliptical galaxies from Siena Galaxy Atlas with filaments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.02062)
*Yuvraj Muralichandran,Noam I. Libeskind,Elmo Tempel*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本研究利用Siena Galaxy Atlas和SDSS-DR12数据，分析椭圆星系和旋涡星系自转轴与宇宙网丝状结构的对齐关系，发现椭圆星系自转轴法线与丝状结构呈显著垂直对齐（高达13σ），而旋涡星系则表现出较弱但非零的对齐信号（约2.8σ），并对不同距离和亮度下的对齐显著性进行了分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 星系的性质受其所处大尺度结构的影响，理论预测星系晕的自转角动量在结构形成的线性阶段获得，因此可能与宇宙网结构存在自旋对齐现象，本研究旨在通过观测数据验证这一预测。

Method: 使用Siena Galaxy Atlas中的最大公开星系目录，结合SDSS-DR12中z ≤ 0.2星系的Bisous方法构建丝状结构，分析32517个盘状星系和18955个椭圆星系在距丝状脊2 Mpc范围内的自转轴与宿主丝状结构的对齐情况，并研究对齐信号随距离和绝对光度的变化。

Result: 椭圆星系的自转轴法线与宿主丝状结构呈强烈垂直对齐（最高达≈13σ），显著偏离随机分布；旋涡星系的自转轴与宿主丝状结构有较弱但非零的对齐信号（≈2.8σ）；对齐信号的显著性随距丝状脊的距离变化，旋涡星系在0.5–1 Mpc处达到最大，椭圆星系在0.2–0.5 Mpc处最大；通过按距离和绝对光度筛选星系可最大化对齐显著性。

Conclusion: 观测结果支持星系角动量获取与大尺度结构形成相关的理论，椭圆星系与丝状结构存在强烈垂直对齐，旋涡星系对齐较弱，表明不同类型星系在结构形成中受到不同的环境影响。

Abstract: The properties of galaxies are known to have been influenced by the
large-scale structures that they inhabit. Theory suggests that galaxies acquire
angular momentum during the linear stage of structure formation, and hence
predict alignments between the spin of halos and the nearby structures of the
cosmic web. In this study, we use the largest catalog of galaxies publicly
available - the Siena Galaxy Atlas - to study the alignment of the spin normals
of elliptical and spiral galaxies with filaments constructed by applying the
Bisous process on galaxies ($z \le$ 0.2) from SDSS - DR12. Our sample comprises
32517 disk and 18955 elliptical galaxies that are within 2 Mpc of any filament
spine. We find that the spin normals of elliptical galaxies exhibit a strong
perpendicular alignment with respect to the orientation of the host filaments,
inconsistent with random distributions by up to $\approx$ 13 $\sigma$. The spin
axis of spiral galaxies shows a much weaker but nonzero alignment signal with
their host filaments of $ \approx$ 2.8$\sigma$ when compared with random. These
numbers depend on exactly how the significance is measured, as elucidated in
the text. Furthermore, the significance of the alignment signal is examined as
a function of distance from the filament spine. Spiral galaxies reach a maximum
signal between 0.5 and 1 Mpc. elliptical galaxies reach their maximum
significance between 0.2 and 0.5 Mpc. We also note that with a tailored
selection of galaxies, as a function of both i) distance from the filaments \&
as a ii) function of absolute luminosity, the alignment significance can be
maximized.

### [220] [Cosmological constraints from the Planck cluster catalogue with DES shear profiles and Chandra observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.02068)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用Chandra X射线数据标定SZ信号与流体静力学质量之间的关系，利用DES弱引力透镜剪切轮廓修正流体静力学质量偏差，并联合PSZ2数密度和BAO数据进行联合拟合。

Result: 基线分析得Ω_m=0.312^{+0.018}_{-0.024}, σ_8=0.777±0.024, S_8=0.791^{+0.023}_{-0.021}, (1-b)=0.844^{+0.055}_{-0.062}；考虑质量依赖的偏差时结果略有变化；与eROSITA结果存在2.9σ张力，但质量校准一致，表明张力源于其他因素。

Abstract: We present cosmological constraints from the Planck PSZ2 cosmological cluster
sample, using weak-lensing shear profiles from Dark Energy Survey (DES) data
and X-ray observations from the Chandra telescope for the mass calibration. We
compute hydrostatic mass estimates for all clusters in the PSZ2 sample with a
scaling relation between their Sunyaev-Zeldovich signal and X-ray derived
hydrostatic mass, calibrated with the Chandra data. We introduce a method to
correct these masses with a hydrostatic mass bias using shear profiles from
wide-field galaxy surveys. We simultaneously fit the number counts of the PSZ2
sample and the mass calibration with the DES data, finding
$\Omega_\text{m}=0.312^{+0.018}_{-0.024}$, $\sigma_8=0.777\pm 0.024$,
$S_8\equiv \sigma_8 \sqrt{\Omega_\text{m} / 0.3}=0.791^{+0.023}_{-0.021}$, and
$(1-b)=0.844^{+0.055}_{-0.062}$ for our baseline analysis when combined with
BAO data. When considering a hydrostatic mass bias evolving with mass, we find
$\Omega_\text{m}=0.353^{+0.025}_{-0.031}$, $\sigma_8=0.751\pm 0.023$, and
$S_8=0.814^{+0.019}_{-0.020}$. We verify the robustness of our results by
exploring a variety of analysis settings, with a particular focus on the
definition of the halo centre used for the extraction of shear profiles. We
compare our results with a number of other analyses, in particular two recent
analyses of cluster samples obtained from SPT and eROSITA data that share the
same mass calibration data set. We find that our results are in overall
agreement with most late-time probes, in very mild tension with CMB results
(1.6$\sigma$), and in significant tension with results from eROSITA clusters
(2.9$\sigma$). We confirm that our mass calibration is consistent with the
eROSITA analysis by comparing masses for clusters present in both Planck and
eROSITA samples, eliminating it as a potential cause of tension.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 线强度映射数据的解释受限于目标谱线与连续谱及来自其他红移的干扰谱线之间的分离困难，且天体物理模型的不确定性使得各成分的相对幅度难以确定。

Method: 采用神经网络方法，在模拟的SPHEREx样数据上训练模型，考虑多频通道间的相关性以及像素级散射和连续谱的影响，实现对目标线、干扰线和连续谱功率谱的分离。

Result: 无连续谱时，目标线功率谱恢复误差在2.5%以内；包含连续谱时，连续谱和目标线的重建误差分别为2%和6%，干扰线则未能有效恢复；降低像素散射可进一步将误差降至1%（连续谱）和3%（目标线）。

Abstract: Line-intensity mapping (LIM) traces the large-scale distribution of matter by
measuring fluctuations in aggregate line emission from unresolved galaxies and
the intergalactic medium, providing a powerful probe of both astrophysics and
cosmology. However, interpreting LIM data is limited by our ability to
disentangle the signal of a target spectral line from continuum emission and
interloper lines, which are emissions from other redshifts that fall within the
observed frequency band. Astrophysical modeling uncertainties further
complicate matters, leaving the relative amplitudes of the map components
poorly understood. In this paper, we present a neural-network (NN) approach to
separate the three map components at the level of the angular power spectrum,
explicitly accounting for uncertainties in their relative amplitudes. As test
cases, we generate SPHEREx-like maps with variable interloper line luminosities
across multiple frequency channels, with and without pixel-wise scatter and
continuum contributions. We find that cross-channel correlations are essential
for robust NN performance when scatter is present. The NN exhibits a hierarchy
in residual errors: brighter components yield smaller residuals, and the
dimmest the highest. Without continuum emission, the network recovers the
target power spectrum to within $2.5\%$, while partially correcting the
interloper spectra. With continuum included, the NN accurately reconstructs the
power spectra of the continuum and target line, within $2\%$ and $6\%$,
respectively, but fails to recover those of the interlopers. Reducing
pixel-level scatter further improves performance, lowering residual errors to
$1\%$ (continuum) and $3\%$ (target line).

### [223] [Can an Anti-de Sitter Vacuum in the Dark Energy Sector Explain JWST High-Redshift Galaxy and Reionization Observations?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.02431)
*Anirban Chakraborty,Tirthankar Roy Choudhury,Anjan Ananda Sen,Purba Mukherjee*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JWST观测到z > 10处存在大量UV明亮星系，与ΛCDM模型预测不符，需检验是否可通过修改宇宙学背景（而非星系物理演化）来解决这一张力。

Method: 采用包含反德西特真空的量子引力启发模型，结合自洽的半解析星系演化与再电离耦合模型，检验该框架对高红移UV光度函数、CMB及低红移观测的符合程度。

Result: 仅拟合高红移UVLF的模型与CMB等低红移观测严重冲突；符合多观测约束的模型对结构形成的增强有限，无法重现JWST观测到的高星系丰度。

Conclusion: 此类仅依赖宇宙学修正的模型不足以解释JWST观测结果，必须引入早期星系的演化性质（如恒星形成效率、尘埃消光等）才能解决早期星系形成难题。

Abstract: The James Webb Space Telescope's (JWST) discovery of an unexpectedly high
abundance of UV-bright galaxies at redshifts $z > 10$ poses a significant
challenge to the standard $\Lambda$CDM cosmology. This work tests whether this
tension can be resolved solely by modifying the cosmological background,
without invoking significant evolution in the astrophysical properties of early
galaxies. We investigate an alternative framework featuring the presence of an
anti-de Sitter vacuum in the dark energy sector, a model that naturally arises
in quantum gravity models like string theory and can enhance early structure
formation. Using a self-consistent semi-analytical model that couples galaxy
evolution with reionization, we confront this scenario with a wide range of
observations. We first show that while a model tailored to fit the high-$z$ UV
luminosity functions (UVLFs) shows promise, it is in strong tension with
well-established cosmological constraints from the CMB and other low-redshift
probes. Conversely, models within this framework that are consistent with these
constraints provide only a modest boost to structure formation and fail to
reproduce the observed JWST galaxy abundances at $z > 10$. While these models
remain consistent with the cosmic reionization history, our primary result is
that this class of cosmological modifications is insufficient on its own to
explain the galaxy excess. Our study underscores the critical importance of
holistic testing for any beyond-$\Lambda$CDM proposal; apparent success in one
observational regime does not guarantee overall viability. By demonstrating the
limitations of a purely cosmological solution, our results strengthen the case
that evolving astrophysical properties are a necessary ingredient for solving
the challenge of early galaxy formation.

### [224] [Kinetic field theory of compact systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.02459)
*Matthias Bartelmann,James Stokes*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文发展了非均匀和各向异性假设下的动力学场论，并在短程相互作用的可解玩具模型中比较了一阶微扰理论与迭代平均场近似，表明平均场理论能保持正定性并捕捉坍塌动力学，从而解析估计爆破时间。在自引力薄层模型中，一阶微扰理论重现了临界现象。该工作为平均场近似的收敛性分析及在更复杂非均匀系统中的应用提供了路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统动力学场论常依赖统计均匀性和各向同性假设，限制了其在非均匀系统中的应用。本文旨在去除这些假设，发展更普适的动力学场论框架，并评估平均场近似在非均匀系统中的有效性。

Method: 采用无统计均匀性和各向同性假设的动力学场论方法，结合一阶微扰理论与迭代平均场近似，在短程相互作用玩具模型和自引力薄层模型中进行对比分析。

Result: 在一阶微扰理论与迭代平均场的比较中，发现后者能保持概率正定性并准确描述坍塌动力学，给出爆破时间的解析估计；在自引力模型中，一阶微扰理论可重现临界现象。

Conclusion: 该研究为非均匀系统的动力学分析提供了新工具，表明平均场理论在描述坍塌等非线性现象方面具有优势，为后续收敛性分析和复杂系统应用奠定了基础。

Abstract: The kinetic field theory is developed without assumptions of statistical
homogeneity and isotropy. In a solvable toy model with short-ranged
interactions, we compare first-order perturbation theory to an iterated
mean-field approximation scheme, demonstrating that the mean-field theory
maintains positivity and captures collapse dynamics, allowing analytic
estimates of blow-up times. In a self-gravitating sheet model, the first-order
perturbation theory is shown to reproduce critical phenomena. This work
suggests a path toward convergence analysis of the mean-field approximation and
applications to more complex inhomogeneous systems.

</details>
